Somanassasampayuttapacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ yassa cittassa anantarā somanassasampayuttapacchimacittaṃ uppajjissati tassa cittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjati upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2333Ms 35Y10_3687« Yassa vā pana yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjatīti?

SC 2334Ms 35Y10_3688Somanassasampayuttapacchimacittassa uppādakkhaṇe yassa cittassa anantarā somanassasampayuttapacchimacittaṃ uppajjissati tassa cittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjati. Somanassasampayuttapacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ yassa cittassa anantarā somanassasampayuttapacchimacittaṃ uppajjissati tassa cittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati somanassindriyañca na uppajjati.

SC 2335Ms 35Y10_3689» Yassa yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjati tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2336Ms 35Y10_3690Sabbesaṃ cittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe somanassavippayuttacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjati, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Somanassasampayuttapacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjati manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2337Ms 35Y10_3691« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjatīti?

SC 2338Ms 35Y10_3692Somanassasampayuttapacchimacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjati. Somanassasampayuttapacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati somanassindriyañca na uppajjati. (Somanassindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2339Ms 35Y10_3693Msdiv 401» Yassa yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjati tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2340Ms 35Y10_3694Sabbesaṃ cittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe upekkhāvippayuttacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjati, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe somanassasampayuttapacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjati manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2341PTS vp Pali 2.182Ms 35Y10_3695« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjatīti?

SC 2342Ms 35Y10_3696Upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjati. Upekkhāsampayuttapacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe somanassasampayuttapacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati upekkhindriyañca na uppajjati. (Upekkhindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2343Ms 35Y10_3697Msdiv 402» Yassa yattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjati tassa tattha paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2344Ms 35Y10_3698Sabbesaṃ cittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe saddhāvippayuttacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjati, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Pacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha saddhindriyañca na uppajjati manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2345Ms 35Y10_3699« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjatīti?

SC 2346Ms 35Y10_3700Pacchimacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjati. Pacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati saddhindriyañca na uppajjati. (Saddhindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2347Ms 35Y10_3701Msdiv 403» Yassa yattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjati tassa tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2348Ms 35Y10_3702Sabbesaṃ cittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe ñāṇavippayuttacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjati, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Pacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha paññindriyañca na uppajjati manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2349Ms 35Y10_3703« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjatīti?

SC 2350Ms 35Y10_3704Pacchimacittassa uppādakkhaṇe tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjati. Pacchimacittassa bhaṅgakkhaṇe asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati paññindriyañca na uppajjati. (Paññindriyamūlakaṃ.)

10.2.1.6. Atītānāgatavāra

10.2.1.6.1. Anulomapuggala

SC 2351PTS vp Pali 2.183Ms 35Y10_3705Msdiv 404» Yassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha tassa sotindriyaṃ uppajjissatīti?

SC 2352Ms 35Y10_3706Pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca arūpaṃ upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ sotindriyaṃ uppajjissati. Itaresaṃ tesaṃ cakkhundriyañca uppajjittha sotindriyañca uppajjissati.

SC 2353Ms 35Y10_3707« Yassa vā pana sotindriyaṃ uppajjissati tassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjitthāti? Āmantā.

SC 2354Ms 35Y10_3708» Yassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha tassa ghānindriyaṃ uppajjissatīti?

SC 2355Ms 35Y10_3709Pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca rūpāvacaraṃ arūpāvacaraṃ upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ ghānindriyaṃ uppajjissati. Itaresaṃ tesaṃ cakkhundriyañca uppajjittha ghānindriyañca uppajjissati.

SC 2356Ms 35Y10_3710« Yassa vā pana ghānindriyaṃ uppajjissati tassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjitthāti? Āmantā.

SC 2357Ms 35Y10_3711» Yassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha tassa itthindriyaṃ uppajjissatīti?

SC 2358Ms 35Y10_3712Pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca rūpāvacaraṃ arūpāvacaraṃ upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti ye ca purisā eteneva bhāvena katici bhave dassetvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ itthindriyaṃ uppajjissati. Itaresaṃ tesaṃ cakkhundriyañca uppajjittha itthindriyañca uppajjissati.

SC 2359Ms 35Y10_3713« Yassa vā pana itthindriyaṃ uppajjissati tassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjitthāti? Āmantā.

SC 2360Ms 35Y10_3714» Yassa cakkhundriyaṃ uppajjittha tassa purisindriyaṃ uppajjissatīti?

SC 2526Ms 35Y10_3880Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ uppajjissati. Itaresaṃ kāmāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyañca uppajjittha manindriyañca uppajjissati.

SC 2528Ms 35Y10_3882Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ uppajjittha. Kāmāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca uppajjissati purisindriyañca uppajjittha. (Purisindriyamūlakaṃ.)

Itaresaṃ catuvokārānaṃ pañcavokārānaṃ tesaṃ tattha jīvitindriyañca uppajjittha somanassindriyañca uppajjissati.

SC 2574Ms 35Y10_3928Msdiv 426» Yassa yattha cakkhundriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha sotindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Āmantā.

SC 2575Ms 35Y10_3929« Yassa vā pana yattha sotindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha cakkhundriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2577Ms 35Y10_3931» Yassa yattha cakkhundriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Āmantā.

SC 2578Ms 35Y10_3932« Yassa vā pana yattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha cakkhundriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2580Ms 35Y10_3934» Yassa yattha cakkhundriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Āmantā.

SC 2590Ms 35Y10_3944» Yassa yattha cakkhundriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Āmantā.

SC 2612Ms 35Y10_3966Rūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyañca na uppajjittha somanassindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2613Ms 35Y10_3967« Yassa vā pana yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2614Ms 35Y10_3968Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca saghānakā upekkhāya upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjissati ghānindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2615Ms 35Y10_3969» Yassa yattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2616Ms 35Y10_3970Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyañca na uppajjittha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2617Ms 35Y10_3971« Yassa vā pana yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2618Ms 35Y10_3972Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca saghānakā somanassena upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati ghānindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2619Ms 35Y10_3973» Yassa yattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2620Ms 35Y10_3974Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyañca na uppajjittha manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2621Ms 35Y10_3975« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2622Ms 35Y10_3976Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha ghānindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati ghānindriyañca na uppajjittha. (Ghānindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2623Ms 35Y10_3977Msdiv 428» Yassa yattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Āmantā.

SC 2624Ms 35Y10_3978« Yassa vā pana yattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2625PTS vp Pali 2.194Ms 35Y10_3979Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ yā ca itthiyo eteneva bhāvena katici bhave dassetvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyañca na uppajjissati itthindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2626Ms 35Y10_3980» Yassa yattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2627Ms 35Y10_3981Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ tesaṃ tattha itthindriyañca na uppajjittha jīvitindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2628Ms 35Y10_3982« Yassa vā pana yattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2629Ms 35Y10_3983Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ tesaṃ tattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ tesaṃ tattha jīvitindriyañca na uppajjissati itthindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2630Ms 35Y10_3984» Yassa yattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2632Ms 35Y10_3986« Yassa vā pana yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2633Ms 35Y10_3987Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ yā ca itthiyo upekkhāya upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjissati itthindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2634Ms 35Y10_3988» Yassa yattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2635Ms 35Y10_3989Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha itthindriyañca na uppajjittha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2636Ms 35Y10_3990« Yassa vā pana yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2637Ms 35Y10_3991Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ yā ca itthiyo somanassena upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati itthindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2638Ms 35Y10_3992» Yassa yattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2640Ms 35Y10_3994« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha itthindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2642Ms 35Y10_3996Msdiv 429» Yassa yattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2644Ms 35Y10_3998« Yassa vā pana yattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2646Ms 35Y10_4000» Yassa yattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2648Ms 35Y10_4002« Yassa vā pana yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2649Ms 35Y10_4003Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca purisā upekkhāya upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ arūpānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjissati purisindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2650Ms 35Y10_4004» Yassa yattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2651Ms 35Y10_4005Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyañca na uppajjittha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2652Ms 35Y10_4006« Yassa vā pana yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2653Ms 35Y10_4007Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ ye ca purisā somanassena upapajjitvā parinibbāyissanti tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati purisindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2654Ms 35Y10_4008» Yassa yattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2655Ms 35Y10_4009Rūpāvacarānaṃ arūpāvacarānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha purisindriyañca na uppajjittha manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2656Ms 35Y10_4010« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2657Ms 35Y10_4011Kāmāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha purisindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Rūpāvacare arūpāvacare pacchimabhavikānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati purisindriyañca na uppajjittha. (Purisindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2658PTS vp Pali 2.195Ms 35Y10_4012Msdiv 430» Yassa yattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Uppajjissati.

SC 2659Ms 35Y10_4013« Yassa vā pana yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti? Uppajjittha.

SC 2660Ms 35Y10_4014» Yassa yattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ … pe … saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti? Uppajjissati.

SC 2661Ms 35Y10_4015« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha jīvitindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti? Uppajjittha. (Jīvitindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2662Ms 35Y10_4016Msdiv 431» Yassa yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2663Ms 35Y10_4017Suddhāvāsānaṃ dutiye citte vattamāne tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjittha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2664Ms 35Y10_4018« Yassa vā pana yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2665Ms 35Y10_4019Pacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ yassa cittassa anantarā somanassasampayuttapacchimacittaṃ uppajjissati tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjissati somanassindriyañca na uppajjittha.

SC 2666Ms 35Y10_4020» Yassa yattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2667Ms 35Y10_4021Suddhāvāsānaṃ dutiye citte vattamāne tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyañca na uppajjittha manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2668Ms 35Y10_4022« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2669Ms 35Y10_4023Pacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha somanassindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati somanassindriyañca na uppajjittha. (Somanassindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2670Ms 35Y10_4024Msdiv 432» Yassa yattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ … pe … paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2671Ms 35Y10_4025Suddhāvāsaṃ upapajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyañca na uppajjittha manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2672PTS vp Pali 2.196Ms 35Y10_4026« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2673Ms 35Y10_4027Pacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha upekkhindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati upekkhindriyañca na uppajjittha. (Upekkhindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2674Ms 35Y10_4028Msdiv 433» Yassa yattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha paññindriyaṃ … pe … manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2675Ms 35Y10_4029Suddhāvāsaṃ upapajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha saddhindriyañca na uppajjittha manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2676Ms 35Y10_4030« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2677Ms 35Y10_4031Pacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha saddhindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati saddhindriyañca na uppajjittha. (Saddhindriyamūlakaṃ.)

SC 2678Ms 35Y10_4032Msdiv 434» Yassa yattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjittha tassa tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissatīti?

SC 2679Ms 35Y10_4033Suddhāvāsaṃ upapajjantānaṃ tesaṃ tattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjittha, no ca tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha paññindriyañca na uppajjittha manindriyañca na uppajjissati.

SC 2680Ms 35Y10_4034« Yassa vā pana yattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati tassa tattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjitthāti?

SC 2681Ms 35Y10_4035Pacchimacittasamaṅgīnaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyaṃ na uppajjissati, no ca tesaṃ tattha paññindriyaṃ na uppajjittha. Asaññasattānaṃ tesaṃ tattha manindriyañca na uppajjissati paññindriyañca na uppajjittha. (Paññindriyamūlakaṃ.) … pe ….
